<pr_description>
Using dynamic styles with StyleX constants from defineConsts
### Describe the issue

When using a dynamic function as a style value in `stylex.create` together with a constants from a StyleX constants file (`defineConsts`), the following error occurs:

```bash
/stylex/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js: Invalid pseudo or at-rule.

      68 |       )
      69 |     ) {
    > 70 |       throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
         |             ^
      71 |     }
      72 |     if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      73 |       throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);

      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:70:13)
      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:42:9)
      at styleXCreateSet (src/shared/stylex-create.js:57:22)
      at transformStyleXCreate (src/visitors/stylex-create.js:169:19)
      at PluginPass.CallExpression (src/index.js:311:30)
      at call (../../../node_modules/@babel/traverse/src/visitors.ts:303:14)

```

### Expected behavior

Correct style transformation using constants as dynamic styles

### Steps to reproduce

Add styles as in `test case` section

### Test case

```js
// packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/transform-stylex-defineConsts-test.js

test('dynamic styles with StyleX constants', () => {
      const { code, } = transformWithInlineConsts(`
        import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
        import { mediaQueries } from './constants.stylex';

        export const styles = stylex.create({
          nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
            transition: {
              [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'none',
              default: \`transform \${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out\`,
            },
          }),
        });
      `);

      expect(code).toMatchInlineSnapshot(`
        "
          // Transformation result
        "
      `);
    });
```

### Additional comments

Thanks to @martinbooth for discovering and [reporting](https://github.com/Dwlad90/stylex-swc-plugin/issues/504) this bug

    10	import * as messages from '../messages';
    11	import { isPlainObject } from '../utils/object-utils';
    12	
    13	export function validateNamespace(
    14	  namespace: mixed,
    15	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    16	): void {
    17	  if (!isPlainObject(namespace)) {
    18	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_NAMESPACE_VALUE);
    19	  }
    20	  const ns: { +[string]: mixed } = namespace;
    21	  for (const key in ns) {
    22	    const val = ns[key];
    23	    if (val === null || typeof val === 'string' || typeof val === 'number') {
    24	      continue;
    25	    }
    26	    if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    27	      for (const v of val) {
    28	        if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    29	          continue;
    30	        }
    31	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_ARRAY_VALUE);
    32	      }
    33	      continue;
    34	    }
    35	    if (isPlainObject(val)) {
    36	      if (key.startsWith('@') || key.startsWith(':')) {
    37	        if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    38	          throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    39	        }
    40	        validateNamespace(val, [...conditions, key]);
    41	      } else {
    42	        validateConditionalStyles(val as $FlowFixMe);
    43	      }
    44	      continue;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    48	  }
    49	}
    50	
    51	type ConditionalStyles = $ReadOnly<{
    52	  [key: string]: string | number | ConditionalStyles,
    53	}>;
    54	
    55	function validateConditionalStyles(
    56	  val: ConditionalStyles,
    57	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    58	): void {
    59	  for (const key in val) {
    60	    const v = val[key];
    61	    if (
    62	      !(
    63	        key.startsWith('@') ||
    64	        key.startsWith(':') ||
    65	        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    66	        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    67	        key === 'default'
    68	      )
    69	    ) {
    70	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    71	    }
    72	    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    73	      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    74	    }
    75	    if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    76	      continue;
    77	    }
    78	    if (Array.isArray(v)) {
    79	      for (const vv of v) {
    80	        if (vv === null || typeof vv === 'string' || typeof vv === 'number') {
    81	          continue;
    82	        }
    83	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    84	      }
    85	      continue;
    86	    }
    87	    if (isPlainObject(v)) {
    88	      validateConditionalStyles(v, [...conditions, key]);
    89	      continue;
    90	    }
    91	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    92	  }
    93	}
    94

    31	// This takes the object of styles passed to `stylex.create` and transforms it.
    32	//   The transformation replaces style values with classNames.
    33	//
    34	// It also collects all injected styles along the way.
    35	// It then returns a tuple of the transformed style Object and an object of injected styles.
    36	//
    37	// This function does some basic validation, and then uses `styleXCreateNamespace` to transform

    39	//
    40	// Before returning, it ensures that there are no duplicate styles being injected.

    43	  options?: StyleXOptions = defaultOptions,
    44	): [

    48	] {
    49	  const resolvedNamespaces: { [string]: FlatCompiledStyles } = {};
    50	  const injectedStyles: { [string]: InjectableStyle } = {};
    51	  const namespaceToClassPaths: { [string]: ClassPathsInNamespace } = {};
    52	
    53	  for (const namespaceName of Object.keys(namespaces)) {
    54	    const namespace = namespaces[namespaceName];
    55	    const classPathsInNamespace: { [string]: $ReadOnlyArray<string> } = {};
    56	
    57	    validateNamespace(namespace);
    58	
    59	    // filterReverse to remove duplicate keys and keep the last one always.
    60	    // This is the same behaviour as Object.fromEntries, except it maintains
    61	    // order correctly and is more efficient.
    62	    const seenProperties = new Set<string>();
    63	    const flattenedNamespace: $ReadOnlyArray<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>> =
    64	      flattenRawStyleObject(namespace, options).reduceRight(
    65	        (arr, curr) => {
    66	          if (seenProperties.has(curr[0])) {
    67	            return arr;
    68	          }
    69	          seenProperties.add(curr[0]);
    70	          arr.unshift(curr);
    71	          return arr;
    72	        },
    73	        [] as Array<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>>,
    74	      );
    75	
    76	    const compiledNamespaceTuples: $ReadOnlyArray<TPropTuple> =
    77	      flattenedNamespace.map(([key, value]) => {
    78	        // Skip variables-as-keys to avoid regression to dynamic styles output
    79	        if (options.enableMinifiedKeys === true && !key.startsWith('--')) {
    80	          const hashedKey = createShortHash('<>' + key);

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *

    10	import type { RawStyles, StyleXOptions, TStyleValue } from '../common-types';
    11	
    12	import flatMapExpandedShorthands from './index';
    13	import { lastMediaQueryWinsTransform } from 'style-value-parser';
    14	import * as messages from '../messages';
    15	
    16	import {
    17	  NullPreRule,
    18	  PreRule,
    19	  PreRuleSet,
    20	  type AnyPreRule,
    21	  type IPreRule,
    22	} from './PreRule';
    23	
    24	export function flattenRawStyleObject(
    25	  style: RawStyles,
    26	  options: StyleXOptions,
    27	): $ReadOnlyArray<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>> {
    28	  let processedStyle = style;
    29	  try {
    30	    processedStyle = options.enableMediaQueryOrder
    31	      ? lastMediaQueryWinsTransform(style)
    32	      : style;
    33	  } catch (error) {
    34	    throw new Error(messages.INVALID_MEDIA_QUERY_SYNTAX);
    35	  }
    36	  return _flattenRawStyleObject(processedStyle, [], options);
    37	}
    38	
    39	export function _flattenRawStyleObject(
    40	  style: RawStyles,
    41	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    42	  options: StyleXOptions,
    43	): Array<$ReadOnly<[string, AnyPreRule]>> {
    44	  const flattened: Array<$ReadOnly<[string, AnyPreRule]>> = [];
    45	  for (const _key in style) {
    46	    const value = style[_key];
    47	    const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
    48	      ? _key.slice(4, -1)
    49	      : _key;
    50	
    51	    // Default styles
    52	    if (
    53	      value === null ||
    54	      typeof value === 'string' ||
    55	      typeof value === 'number'
    56	    ) {
    57	      const pairs: $ReadOnlyArray<[string, TStyleValue]> =
    58	        flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, value], options);
    59	      for (const [property, value] of pairs) {
    60	        if (value === null) {
    61	          flattened.push([property, new NullPreRule()]);
    62	        } else {
    63	          flattened.push([
    64	            property,
    65	            new PreRule(
    66	              property,
    67	              value,
    68	              keyPath.includes(key)
    69	                ? keyPath.map((k) => (k === key ? property : k))
    70	                : [...keyPath, property],
    71	            ),
    72	          ]);
    73	        }
    74	      }
    75	      continue;
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    // Fallback Styles
    79	    if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    80	      // Step 1: Expand properties to its constituent parts
    81	      // Collect the various values for each value in the array
    82	      // that belongs to the same property.
    83	      const equivalentPairs: {
    84	        [string]: Array<null | string | number>,
    85	      } = {};
    86	      for (const eachVal of value) {
    87	        const pairs = flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, eachVal], options);
    88	        for (const [property, val] of pairs) {
    89	          if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    90	            if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
    91	              equivalentPairs[property] = [...val];
    92	            } else {
    93	              equivalentPairs[property].push(...val);
    94	            }
    95	          } else if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
    96	            equivalentPairs[property] = [val];
    97	          } else {
    98	            equivalentPairs[property].push(val);
    99	          }
   100	        }
   101	      }
   102	      // Deduplicate
   103	      Object.entries(equivalentPairs)
   104	        // Remove Nulls
   105	        .map(([property, values]) => [
   106	          property,
   107	          [...new Set(values.filter(Boolean))],
   108	        ])
   109	        // Deduplicate and default to null when no values are found
   110	        .map(([property, values]) => [
   111	          property,
   112	          values.length === 0 ? null : values.length === 1 ? values[0] : values,
   113	        ])
   114	        // Push to flattened
   115	        .forEach(([property, value]) => {
   116	          if (value === null) {
   117	            flattened.push([property, new NullPreRule()]);
   118	          } else {
   119	            flattened.push([
   120	              property,
   121	              new PreRule(
   122	                property,
   123	                value,
   124	                keyPath.includes(_key)
   125	                  ? keyPath.map((k) => (k === _key ? property : k))
   126	                  : [...keyPath, property],
   127	              ),
   128	            ]);
   129	          }
   130	        });
   131	      continue;
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    // Object Values for properties. e.g. { color: { hover: 'red', default: 'blue' } }
   135	    if (
   136	      typeof value === 'object' &&
   137	      !key.startsWith(':') &&
   138	      !key.startsWith('@')
   139	    ) {
   140	      const equivalentPairs: { [string]: { [string]: AnyPreRule } } = {};
   141	      for (const condition in value) {
   142	        const innerValue = value[condition];
   143	
   144	        const pairs = _flattenRawStyleObject(
   145	          { [key]: innerValue },
   146	          keyPath.length > 0 ? [...keyPath, condition] : [key, condition],
   147	          options,
   148	        );
   149	        for (const [property, preRule] of pairs) {
   150	          if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
   151	            equivalentPairs[property] = { [condition]: preRule };
   152	          } else {
   153	            equivalentPairs[property][condition] = preRule;
   154	          }
   155	        }
   156	      }
   157	      for (const [property, obj] of Object.entries(equivalentPairs)) {
   158	        const sortedKeys = Object.keys(obj); //.sort();
   159	        const rules: Array<AnyPreRule> = [];
   160	        for (const condition of sortedKeys) {
   161	          rules.push(obj[condition]);
   162	        }
   163	        // If there are many conditions with `null` values, we will collapse them into a single `null` value.
   164	        // `PreRuleSet.create` takes care of that for us.
   165	        flattened.push([property, PreRuleSet.create(rules)]);
   166	      }
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    // Object Values for pseudos and at-rules. e.g. { ':hover': { color: 'red' } }
   170	    if (
   171	      typeof value === 'object' &&
   172	      (key.startsWith(':') || key.startsWith('@'))
   173	    ) {
   174	      const pairs = _flattenRawStyleObject(value, [...keyPath, _key], options);
   175	      for (const [property, preRule] of pairs) {
   176	        flattened.push([key + '_' + property, preRule]);
   177	      }
   178	    }
   179	  }
   180	  return flattened;
   181	}
   182

    14	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    15	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';

    17	  create as stylexCreate,
    18	  firstThatWorks as stylexFirstThatWorks,
    19	  keyframes as stylexKeyframes,
    20	  positionTry as stylexPositionTry,
    21	} from '../shared';
    22	import { addSourceMapData } from '../utils/add-sourcemap-data';
    23	import {
    24	  convertToTestStyles,
    25	  injectDevClassNames,
    26	} from '../utils/dev-classname';
    27	import {
    28	  convertObjectToAST,
    29	  removeObjectsWithSpreads,
    30	} from '../utils/js-to-ast';
    31	import { messages } from '../shared';
    32	import { evaluateStyleXCreateArg } from './parse-stylex-create-arg';
    33	import flatMapExpandedShorthands from '../shared/preprocess-rules';
    34	import { hoistExpression, pathReplaceHoisted } from '../utils/ast-helpers';
    35	
    36	function isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr: t.Expression): boolean {
    37	  if (t.isTemplateLiteral(expr)) return true;
    38	
    39	  if (
    40	    t.isStringLiteral(expr) ||
    41	    t.isNumericLiteral(expr) ||
    42	    t.isBooleanLiteral(expr)
    43	  )
    44	    return true;
    45	
    46	  if (t.isBinaryExpression(expr)) {
    47	    return ['+', '-', '*', '/', '%', '**'].includes(expr.operator);
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  if (t.isUnaryExpression(expr)) {
    51	    return ['-', '+'].includes(expr.operator);
    52	  }
    53	
    54	  if (t.isConditionalExpression(expr)) {
    55	    return (
    56	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.consequent) &&
    57	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.alternate)
    58	    );
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  if (t.isLogicalExpression(expr)) {
    62	    if (expr.operator === '??' || expr.operator === '||') {
    63	      return (
    64	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) || isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    65	      );
    66	    }
    67	    if (expr.operator === '&&') {
    68	      return (
    69	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) && isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    70	      );
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  return false;
    75	}
    76	
    77	/// This function looks for `stylex.create` calls and transforms them.
    78	/// 1. It finds the first argument to `stylex.create` and validates it.
    79	/// 2. It pre-processes valid-dynamic parts of style object such as custom presets (spreads)
    80	/// 3. It evaluates the style object to get a JS object. This also handles local constants automatically.
    81	/// 4. It uses the `stylexCreate` from `@stylexjs/shared` to transform the JS
    82	///    object and to get a list of injected styles.
    83	/// 5. It converts the resulting Object back into an AST and replaces the call with it.
    84	/// 6. It also inserts `stylex.inject` calls above the current statement as needed.
    85	export default function transformStyleXCreate(
    86	  path: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    87	  state: StateManager,
    88	) {
    89	  const { node } = path;
    90	
    91	  if (node.type !== 'CallExpression') {
    92	    return;
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  if (
    96	    (node.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    97	      state.stylexCreateImport.has(node.callee.name)) ||

   117	
   118	function evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   119	  path: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression>,
   120	  traversalState: StateManager,
   121	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
   122	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
   123	): $ReadOnly<{
   124	  confident: boolean,
   125	  value: any,
   126	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
   127	  reason?: string,
   128	  inlineStyles?: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
   129	}> {
   130	  const obj: { [string]: mixed } = {};
   131	  const inlineStyles: TInlineStyles = {};
   132	  const props: $ReadOnlyArray<
   133	    NodePath<t.ObjectMethod | t.ObjectProperty | t.SpreadElement>,
   134	  > = path.get('properties');
   135	  for (const prop of props) {
   136	    if (prop.isObjectMethod()) {
   137	      return { value: null, confident: false };
   138	    }
   139	    if (prop.isSpreadElement()) {
   140	      const result = evaluate(prop.get('argument'), traversalState, functions);
   141	      if (!result.confident) {
   142	        return result;
   143	      }
   144	      Object.assign(obj, result.value);
   145	      continue;
   146	    }
   147	    if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
   148	      const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(prop, traversalState, functions);
   149	      if (!keyResult.confident) {
   150	        return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
   151	      }
   152	      let key = keyResult.value;
   153	      if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
   154	        key = key.slice(4, -1);
   155	      }
   156	
   157	      const valuePath: NodePath<t.Expression | t.PatternLike> =
   158	        prop.get('value');
   159	
   160	      if (valuePath.isObjectExpression()) {
   161	        const result = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   162	          valuePath,
   163	          traversalState,
   164	          functions,
   165	          [...keyPath, key],
   166	        );
   167	        if (!result.confident) {
   168	          return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt, value: null };
   169	        }
   170	        obj[key] = result.value;
   171	        Object.assign(inlineStyles, result.inlineStyles);
   172	      } else {
   173	        const result = evaluate(valuePath, traversalState, functions);
   174	        if (!result.confident) {
   175	          const fullKeyPath = [...keyPath, key];
   176	          const varName =
   177	            '--x-' +
   178	            (keyPath.length > 0
   179	              ? utils.hash([...keyPath, key].join('_'))
   180	              : key);
   181	          obj[key] = `var(${varName})`;
   182	          const node = valuePath.node;
   183	          if (!t.isExpression(node)) {
   184	            throw valuePath.buildCodeFrameError(
   185	              'Expected expression as style value',
   186	              SyntaxError,
   187	            );
   188	          }
   189	          const expression: t.Expression = node as $FlowFixMe;
   190	
   191	          const propName =
   192	            fullKeyPath.find(
   193	              (k) =>
   194	                !k.startsWith(':') && !k.startsWith('@') && k !== 'default',
   195	            ) ?? key;
   196	
   197	          const unit =
   198	            timeUnits.has(propName) || lengthUnits.has(propName)
   199	              ? getNumberSuffix(propName)
   200	              : '';
   201	
   202	          const inlineStyleExpression =
   203	            unit !== ''
   204	              ? t.callExpression(
   205	                  t.arrowFunctionExpression(
   206	                    [t.identifier('val')],
   207	                    t.conditionalExpression(
   208	                      t.binaryExpression(
   209	                        '===',
   210	                        t.unaryExpression('typeof', t.identifier('val')),
   211	                        t.stringLiteral('number'),
   212	                      ),
   213	                      t.binaryExpression(
   214	                        '+',
   215	                        t.identifier('val'),
   216	                        t.stringLiteral(unit),
   217	                      ),
   218	                      t.conditionalExpression(
   219	                        t.binaryExpression(
   220	                          '!=',
   221	                          t.identifier('val'),
   222	                          t.nullLiteral(),
   223	                        ),
   224	                        t.identifier('val'),
   225	                        t.identifier('undefined'),
   226	                      ),
   227	                    ),
   228	                  ),
   229	                  [expression as t.Expression],
   230	                )
   231	              : t.conditionalExpression(
   232	                  t.binaryExpression('!=', expression, t.nullLiteral()),
   233	                  expression,
   234	                  t.identifier('undefined'),
   235	                );
   236	          inlineStyles[varName] = {
   237	            path: [...keyPath, key],
   238	            originalExpression: expression,
   239	            expression: inlineStyleExpression,
   240	          };
   241	        } else {
   242	          obj[key] = result.value;
   243	        }
   244	      }
   245	    }
   246	  }
   247	  return { value: obj, confident: true, inlineStyles };
   248	}
   249	
   250	type KeyResult =
   251	  | { confident: true, value: string }
   252	  | { confident: false, deopt?: null | NodePath<> };
   253	
   254	function evaluateObjKey(
   255	  prop: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty>,
   256	  traversalState: StateManager,
   257	  functions: FunctionConfig,
   258	): KeyResult {
   259	  const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   260	  let key: string;
   261	  if ((prop.node as t.ObjectProperty).computed) {
   262	    const result = evaluate(keyPath, traversalState, functions);
   263	    if (!result.confident) {
   264	      return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt };
   265	    }
   266	    key = result.value;
   267	  } else if (keyPath.isIdentifier()) {
   268	    key = keyPath.node.name;
   269	  } else {
   270	    // TODO: This is'nt handling all possible types that `keyPath` could be
   271	    key = (keyPath.node as $FlowFixMe).value;
   272	  }
   273	  return {
   274	    confident: true,
   275	    value: String(key),
   276	  };
   277	}
   278	
   279	function validateDynamicStyleParams(
   280	  path: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression>,
   281	  params: Array<NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>>,
   282	) {
   283	  if (params.some((param) => !param.isIdentifier())) {
   284	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   285	      messages.ONLY_NAMED_PARAMETERS_IN_DYNAMIC_STYLE_FUNCTIONS,
   286	      SyntaxError,
   287	    );
   288	  }
   289	}
   290

Now I understand the issue better. When we have a dynamic function with StyleX constants (like `breakpoints.small`), the code evaluates the constants and replaces them with their values. However, in the `evaluateObjKey` function (lines 254-277), when it encounters a computed property key with a constant from `defineConsts`, it returns the actual value (e.g., `"@media (max-width: 600px)"`) instead of keeping it as a placeholder variable like `var(--x1r2wpmh)`.

The issue is that when these constants are evaluated, they need to be treated like other constants from `defineConsts` and be replaced with a placeholder. Let me look at how constants are normally handled:

    10	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';
    11	
    12	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    13	import { evaluate } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    14	import { utils, defineConsts as styleXDefineConsts, messages } from '../shared';
    15	import { convertObjectToAST } from '../utils/js-to-ast';
    16	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';
    17	
    18	/// This function looks for `stylex.defineConsts` calls and transforms them.
    19	/// 1. It finds and validates the first argument to `stylex.defineConsts`.
    20	/// 2. It evaluates the style const object to a JS value, erroring on non-static or non-object values.
    21	/// 3. It generates a theme name from the filename and export name for hashing.
    22	/// 4. It invokes `stylexDefineConsts` to transform the JS object and collect injected styles.
    23	/// 5. It creates a map of key-value pairs of constants to be inlined.
    24	/// 6. It replaces the call with the transformed AST and registers the styles in state.
    25	export default function transformStyleXDefineConsts(
    26	  callExpressionPath: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    27	  state: StateManager,
    28	) {
    29	  const callExpressionNode = callExpressionPath.node;
    30	  if (callExpressionNode.type !== 'CallExpression') return;
    31	
    32	  if (
    33	    (callExpressionNode.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    34	      state.stylexDefineConstsImport.has(callExpressionNode.callee.name)) ||
    35	    (callExpressionNode.callee.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    36	      callExpressionNode.callee.property.name === 'defineConsts' &&
    37	      callExpressionNode.callee.object.type === 'Identifier' &&
    38	      state.stylexImport.has(callExpressionNode.callee.object.name))
    39	  ) {
    40	    validateStyleXDefineConsts(callExpressionPath);
    41	
    42	    const variableDeclaratorPath = callExpressionPath.parentPath;
    43	    if (!variableDeclaratorPath.isVariableDeclarator()) return;
    44	
    45	    const variableDeclaratorNode = variableDeclaratorPath.node;
    46	    if (variableDeclaratorNode.id.type !== 'Identifier') return;
    47	
    48	    const varId: t.Identifier = variableDeclaratorNode.id;
    49	    const args = callExpressionPath.get('arguments');
    50	    const firstArg = args[0];
    51	
    52	    const { confident, value } = evaluate(firstArg, state);
    53	    if (!confident) {
    54	      throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
    55	        messages.nonStaticValue('defineConsts'),
    56	        SyntaxError,
    57	      );
    58	    }
    59	    if (typeof value !== 'object' || value == null) {
    60	      throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
    61	        messages.nonStyleObject('defineConsts'),
    62	        SyntaxError,
    63	      );
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    const fileName = state.fileNameForHashing;
    67	    if (fileName == null) {
    68	      throw new Error(messages.cannotGenerateHash('defineConsts'));
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    const exportName = varId.name;
    72	    const exportId = utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName });
    73	
    74	    const [transformedJsOutput, jsOutput] = styleXDefineConsts(value, {
    75	      ...state.options,
    76	      exportId,
    77	    });
    78	
    79	    callExpressionPath.replaceWith(convertObjectToAST(transformedJsOutput));
    80	
    81	    const styles = Object.entries(jsOutput).map(([_, obj]) => [
    82	      obj.constKey,
    83	      {
    84	        constKey: obj.constKey,
    85	        constVal: obj.constVal,
    86	        ltr: obj.ltr,
    87	        rtl: obj.rtl ?? null,
    88	      },
    89	      obj.priority,
    90	    ]);
    91	
    92	    state.registerStyles(styles);
    93	  }
    94	}
    95	
    96	function validateStyleXDefineConsts(
    97	  callExpressionPath: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    98	) {
    99	  const variableDeclaratorPath = callExpressionPath.parentPath;
   100	  const exportNamedDeclarationPath =
   101	    variableDeclaratorPath.parentPath?.parentPath;
   102	
   103	  if (
   104	    variableDeclaratorPath == null ||
   105	    !variableDeclaratorPath.isVariableDeclarator() ||
   106	    variableDeclaratorPath.node.id.type !== 'Identifier'
   107	  ) {
   108	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   109	      messages.unboundCallValue('defineConsts'),
   110	      SyntaxError,
   111	    );
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  if (
   115	    exportNamedDeclarationPath == null ||
   116	    !exportNamedDeclarationPath.isExportNamedDeclaration()
   117	  ) {
   118	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   119	      messages.nonExportNamedDeclaration('defineConsts'),
   120	      SyntaxError,
   121	    );
   122	  }
   123	
   124	  if (callExpressionPath.node.arguments.length !== 1) {
   125	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   126	      messages.illegalArgumentLength('defineConsts', 1),
   127	      SyntaxError,
   128	    );
   129	  }
   130	}

    10	/**
    11	 * This is a extended version of the path evaluation code from Babel.
    12	 *
    13	 * The original can be found at:
    14	 * https://github.com/babel/babel/blob/main/packages/babel-traverse/src/path/evaluation.ts
    15	 *
    16	 * The following extensions were made:
    17	 * - It can accept a mapping from variable names to functions
    18	 *   which when encountered will be evaluated instead of deopting.
    19	 *   - The functions can be configured to accept the raw path instead of
    20	 *     static values to handle dynamic values.
    21	 * - It can handle object spreads when the spread value itself is statically evaluated.
    22	 */
    23	
    24	import type { NodePath, Binding } from '@babel/traverse';
    25	
    26	import { parseSync } from '@babel/core';
    27	import traverse from '@babel/traverse';
    28	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    29	import StateManager from './state-manager';
    30	import { utils } from '../shared';
    31	import * as errMsgs from './evaluation-errors';
    32	
    33	// This file contains Babels metainterpreter that can evaluate static code.
    34	
    35	const VALID_CALLEES = ['String', 'Number', 'Math', 'Object', 'Array'];
    36	const INVALID_METHODS = [
    37	  'random',
    38	  'assign',
    39	  'defineProperties',
    40	  'defineProperty',
    41	  'freeze',
    42	  'seal',
    43	  'splice',
    44	];
    45	
    46	function isValidCallee(val: string): boolean {
    47	  return (VALID_CALLEES as $ReadOnlyArray<string>).includes(val);
    48	}
    49	
    50	function isInvalidMethod(val: string): boolean {
    51	  return INVALID_METHODS.includes(val);
    52	}
    53	
    54	export type FunctionConfig = {
    55	  identifiers: {
    56	    [fnName: string]: $FlowFixMe,
    57	  },
    58	  memberExpressions: {
    59	    [key: string]: {
    60	      [memberName: string]: {
    61	        fn: (...args: $FlowFixMe[]) => $FlowFixMe,
    62	        takesPath?: boolean,
    63	      },
    64	    },
    65	  },
    66	};
    67	
    68	type State = {
    69	  confident: boolean,
    70	  deoptPath: NodePath<> | null,
    71	  deoptReason?: string,
    72	  seen: Map<t.Node, Result>,
    73	  addedImports: Set<string>,
    74	  functions: FunctionConfig,
    75	  traversalState: StateManager,
    76	};
    77	
    78	type Result =
    79	  | {
    80	      resolved: true,
    81	      value: any,
    82	    }
    83	  | {
    84	      resolved: false,
    85	      reason: string,
    86	    };
    87	/**
    88	 * Deopts the evaluation
    89	 */
    90	function deopt(path: NodePath<>, state: State, reason: string): void {
    91	  if (!state.confident) return;
    92	  state.deoptPath = path;
    93	  state.confident = false;
    94	  state.deoptReason = reason;
    95	}

    98	  filePath: string,
    99	  namedExport: string,
   100	  state: State,

   161	function evaluateThemeRef(
   162	  fileName: string,
   163	  exportName: string,
   164	  state: State,
   165	): { [key: string]: string } {
   166	  const resolveKey = (key: string) => {
   167	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
   168	      return `var(${key})`;
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    const strToHash =
   172	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   173	        ? utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName })
   174	        : utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName, key });
   175	
   176	    const { debug, enableDebugClassNames } = state.traversalState.options;
   177	
   178	    const varSafeKey =
   179	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   180	        ? ''
   181	        : (key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key).replace(
   182	            /[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,
   183	            '_',
   184	          ) + '-';
   185	
   186	    const varName =
   187	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
   188	        ? varSafeKey +
   189	          state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix +
   190	          utils.hash(strToHash)
   191	        : state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix + utils.hash(strToHash);
   192	
   193	    if (key === '__varGroupHash__') {
   194	      return varName;
   195	    }
   196	    return `var(--${varName})`;
   197	  };

   217	/**
   218	 * We wrap the _evaluate method so we can track `seen` nodes, we push an item
   219	 * to the map before we actually evaluate it so we can deopt on self recursive
   220	 * nodes such as:
   221	 *
   222	 *   var g = a ? 1 : 2,
   223	 *       a = g * this.foo
   224	 */
   225	function evaluateCached(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   226	  const { node } = path;
   227	  const { seen } = state;
   228	
   229	  const existing: ?Result = seen.get(node);
   230	  if (existing != null) {
   231	    if (existing.resolved) {
   232	      return existing.value;
   233	    } else {
   234	      deopt(path, state, existing.reason);
   235	      return;
   236	    }
   237	  } else {
   238	    const item: Result = { resolved: false, reason: 'Currently evaluating' };
   239	    seen.set(node, item);
   240	
   241	    if (node == null) {
   242	      deopt(path, state, errMsgs.PATH_WITHOUT_NODE);
   243	      return;
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    const val = _evaluate(path, state);
   247	    if (state.confident) {
   248	      seen.set(node, {
   249	        resolved: true,
   250	        value: val,
   251	      });
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    return val;
   255	  }
   256	}
   257	
   258	function _evaluate(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   259	  if (!state.confident) return;
   260	
   261	  if (path.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
   262	    const body = path.get('body');
   263	    const params: $ReadOnlyArray<
   264	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   265	    > = path.get('params');
   266	    const identParams = params
   267	      .filter(
   268	        (
   269	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   270	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
   271	      )
   272	      .map((paramPath) => paramPath.node.name);
   273	    if (body.isExpression() && identParams.length === params.length) {
   274	      const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = body;
   275	      return (...args) => {
   276	        const identifierEntries = identParams.map(
   277	          (ident, index): [string, any] => [ident, args[index]],
   278	        );
   279	        const identifiersObj = Object.fromEntries(identifierEntries);
   280	        const result = evaluate(expr, state.traversalState, {
   281	          ...state.functions,
   282	          identifiers: { ...state.functions.identifiers, ...identifiersObj },
   283	        });
   284	        return result.value;
   285	      };
   286	    }
   287	  }
   288	
   289	  if (path.isIdentifier()) {
   290	    const name: string = path.node.name;
   291	    if (Object.keys(state.functions?.identifiers ?? {}).includes(name)) {
   292	      return state.functions.identifiers[name];
   293	    }
   294	  }
   295	
   296	  if (path.isTSAsExpression()) {
   297	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = path.get('expression');
   298	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  if (path.node.type === 'TSSatisfiesExpression') {
   302	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = (path as $FlowFixMe).get('expression');
   303	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   304	  }
   305	
   306	  if (path.isSequenceExpression()) {
   307	    const exprs = path.get('expressions');
   308	    return evaluateCached(exprs[exprs.length - 1], state);
   309	  }
   310	
   311	  if (
   312	    path.isStringLiteral() ||
   313	    path.isNumericLiteral() ||
   314	    path.isBooleanLiteral()
   315	  ) {
   316	    return path.node.value;
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  if (path.isNullLiteral()) {
   320	    return null;
   321	  }
   322	
   323	  if (path.isTemplateLiteral()) {
   324	    return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasis, state);
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  const maybeTag = path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() && path.get('tag');
   328	  if (
   329	    path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() &&
   330	    maybeTag &&
   331	    maybeTag.isMemberExpression()
   332	  ) {
   333	    const tag: NodePath<t.MemberExpression> = maybeTag;
   334	    const object: NodePath<t.Expression | t.Super> = tag.get('object');
   335	
   336	    if (object.isIdentifier()) {
   337	      const name = object.node.name;
   338	      const property: NodePath<> = tag.get('property');
   339	
   340	      if (
   341	        name === 'String' &&
   342	        !path.scope.hasBinding(name) &&
   343	        property.isIdentifier() &&
   344	        property.node.name === 'raw'
   345	      ) {
   346	        return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasi.quasis, state, true);
   347	      }
   348	    }
   349	  }

    10	import * as messages from '../messages';
    11	import { isPlainObject } from '../utils/object-utils';
    12	
    13	export function validateNamespace(
    14	  namespace: mixed,
    15	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    16	): void {
    17	  if (!isPlainObject(namespace)) {
    18	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_NAMESPACE_VALUE);
    19	  }
    20	  const ns: { +[string]: mixed } = namespace;
    21	  for (const key in ns) {
    22	    const val = ns[key];
    23	    if (val === null || typeof val === 'string' || typeof val === 'number') {
    24	      continue;
    25	    }
    26	    if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    27	      for (const v of val) {
    28	        if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    29	          continue;
    30	        }
    31	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_ARRAY_VALUE);
    32	      }
    33	      continue;
    34	    }
    35	    if (isPlainObject(val)) {
    36	      if (key.startsWith('@') || key.startsWith(':')) {
    37	        if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    38	          throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    39	        }
    40	        validateNamespace(val, [...conditions, key]);
    41	      } else {
    42	        validateConditionalStyles(val as $FlowFixMe);
    43	      }
    44	      continue;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    48	  }
    49	}

I see the issue now! When we have a property like `transition` with a nested object value, if the key doesn't start with `@` or `:`, it calls `validateConditionalStyles` (line 42). But `validateConditionalStyles` expects the keys in THAT object to start with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or be `default`.

The problem is that in `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively`, when we evaluate the key `[breakpoints.small]`, it returns the actual value `"@media (max-width: 600px)"`, but by the time it reaches `validateNamespace`, the object looks like:

```javascript
{
  transition: {
    "@media (max-width: 600px)": "none",
    "default": "transform ${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out"
  }
}
```

So when `validateNamespace` is called on the top-level object:
1. It sees `transition` key (line 21)
2. The value is an object (line 35)
3. `transition` doesn't start with `@` or `:` (line 36), so it goes to line 42
4. `validateConditionalStyles` is called on that inner object
5. Inside `validateConditionalStyles`, it checks the key `"@media (max-width: 600px)"`
6. The problem: `"@media (max-width: 600px)"` does start with `@`, so it should pass the check on line 63

Wait, let me re-read the validation code. Oh! I see it now. The check on line 63 is:

```javascript
!(
  key.startsWith('@') ||
  key.startsWith(':') ||
  key.startsWith('var(--') ||
  key === 'default'
)
```

The negation `!` means "if the key does NOT start with @, :, var(--, or equal default, then throw error". So a key that starts with `@` SHOULD pass this check.

Let me trace through this more carefully. The object being validated should have the structure:

```javascript
{
  nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
    transition: {
      [breakpoints.small]: 'none',
      default: `transform ${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out`,
    },
  })
}
```

#!/usr/bin/env node

const path = require('path');
const { transformSync } = require('@babel/core');

// Patch the validateNamespace function to see what's being validated
const Module = require('module');
const originalRequire = Module.prototype.require;

Module.prototype.require = function(id) {
  const module = originalRequire.apply(this, arguments);
  
  if (id.includes('basic-validation')) {
    const originalValidateNamespace = module.validateNamespace;
    module.validateNamespace = function(namespace, conditions = []) {
      console.log('validateNamespace called with:');
      console.log('namespace:', JSON.stringify(namespace, null, 2));
      console.log('conditions:', conditions);
      console.log('---');
      return originalValidateNamespace.call(this, namespace, conditions);
    };
  }
  
  return module;
};

const stylexPlugin = require('./packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/lib/index');

function transformWithInlineConsts(source, opts = {}) {
  const { code, metadata } = transformSync(source, {
    filename: path.join(__dirname, 'packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js'),
    parserOpts: { sourceType: 'module' },
    babelrc: false,
    plugins: [
      [
        stylexPlugin,
        {
          ...opts,
          unstable_moduleResolution: {
            rootDir: path.join(__dirname, 'packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__'),
            type: 'commonJS',
          },
        },
      ],
    ],
  });

  return { code, metadata };
}

console.log('Testing dynamic styles with StyleX constants...\n');

try {
  const { code } = transformWithInlineConsts(`
    import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
    import { breakpoints } from './constants.stylex';

    export const styles = stylex.create({
      nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
        transition: {
          [breakpoints.small]: 'none',
          default: \`transform \${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out\`,
        },
      }),
    });
  `);

  console.log('SUCCESS! Code transformed:');
  console.log(code);
} catch (error) {
  console.log('ERROR!');
  console.error(error.message);
}

Perfect! Now I can see the problem clearly:

The key is `"--x1r2wpmh"`, which is just `--x1r2wpmh` without the `var()` wrapper! The code checks for `key.startsWith('var(--')`, but the actual key is just `--x1r2wpmh`.

Looking at the code in `flatten-raw-style-obj.js`, lines 47-49:

```javascript
const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
  ? _key.slice(4, -1)
  : _key;
```

This code strips the `var()` wrapper from the key! So when a key like `var(--x1r2wpmh)` is encountered, it's transformed to just `--x1r2wpmh`.

The validation code in `basic-validation.js` line 66 checks for `key.startsWith('var(--')`, but after the flattening process, the key no longer has the `var()` wrapper.

So the fix is to also check if the key starts with `--` in the validation code. Let me check if there are CSS variable names that can start with `--`:

    24	// The classes in this file are used to represent objects that
    25	// can be compiled into one or CSS rules.
    26	//
    27	// These are thin wrappers around the "values" in Raw Style Objects
    28	// with all the metadata needed to compile them into CSS.
    29	export interface IPreRule {
    30	  compiled(options: StyleXOptions): $ReadOnlyArray<ComputedStyle>;
    31	  equals(other: IPreRule): boolean;
    32	}
    33	
    34	export type AnyPreRule = NullPreRule | PreRule | PreRuleSet;
    35	
    36	export class NullPreRule implements IPreRule {
    37	  compiled(_options: StyleXOptions): [null] {
    38	    return [null];
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  equals(other: IPreRule): boolean {
    42	    return other instanceof NullPreRule;
    43	  }
    44	}
    45	
    46	export class PreRule implements IPreRule {
    47	  +property: string;
    48	  +value: string | number | $ReadOnlyArray<string | number>;
    49	  +keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string>;
    50	
    51	  constructor(
    52	    property: string,
    53	    value: string | number | $ReadOnlyArray<string | number>,
    54	    keyPath?: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    55	  ) {
    56	    this.property = property;
    57	    this.keyPath = keyPath ?? [];
    58	    this.value = value;
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  get pseudos(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
    62	    const unsortedPseudos = this.keyPath.filter((key) => key.startsWith(':'));
    63	    return sortPseudos(unsortedPseudos);
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  get atRules(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
    67	    const unsortedAtRules = this.keyPath.filter((key) => key.startsWith('@'));
    68	    return sortAtRules(unsortedAtRules);
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  get constRules(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
    72	    // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    73	    return this.keyPath.filter((key) => key.startsWith('var(--'));
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  compiled(
    77	    options: StyleXOptions,
    78	  ): $ReadOnlyArray<[string, InjectableStyle, ClassesToOriginalPaths]> {
    79	    const [_key, className, rule] = convertStyleToClassName(
    80	      [this.property, this.value],
    81	      this.pseudos ?? [],
    82	      this.atRules ?? [],
    83	      this.constRules ?? [],
    84	      options,
    85	    );
    86	
    87	    return [[className, rule, { [className]: this.keyPath }]];
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  equals(other: IPreRule): boolean {
    91	    if (!(other instanceof PreRule)) {
    92	      return false;
    93	    }
    94	
    95	    const valuesEqual =
    96	      Array.isArray(this.value) && Array.isArray(other.value)
    97	        ? arrayEquals(this.value, other.value)
    98	        : this.value === other.value;

Wait, but this might be too broad. CSS variables used directly as property names (like `--my-custom-var: value;`) would also match this pattern. Let me check if that's an issue. Looking at the keyPath, it contains the path of keys that led to this rule. So if we have:

```javascript
{
  color: {
    '@media': 'red',
    '--x123': 'blue'  // This is a defineConsts placeholder key (condition)
  }
}
```

The keyPath would be `['color', '--x123']` for the blue value. But if we have:

```javascript
{
  '--my-custom-var': 'red'  // This is a CSS variable property
}
```

The keyPath would be `['--my-custom-var']` for the red value.

So both cases would have `--` in the keyPath. But the difference is:
1. In the first case (defineConsts placeholder), `--x123` is NOT a CSS property name, it's a placeholder condition key
2. In the second case, `--my-custom-var` IS a CSS property name

The problem is that the PreRule doesn't distinguish between these two cases. Let me look at how the code determines whether a key is a property or a condition:

Looking back at the flatten-raw-style-obj.js code:
- Line 47-49: When a key matches `var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)`, it strips the `var()` wrapper
- Line 145: When recursively calling `_flattenRawStyleObject` for conditions, the keyPath includes the condition key

So the question is: can a CSS variable property name (like `--my-var`) end up in the keyPath as a condition? Let's trace through the code:

1. If we have `{ "--my-var": "value" }`, this is a CSS property assignment
2. Line 52-75: If the value is a string/number, it's processed as a property-value pair
3. Line 58: `flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, value], options)` is called
4. The keyPath used here would be `[..., property]` where property is the expanded property name

So CSS variable properties should be fine - they get processed as properties, not as conditions in the keyPath.

Now let's think about defineConsts placeholders:
1. When we have `{ color: { 'var(--x123)': 'red' } }`
2. Line 47-49: The key becomes `--x123` after stripping
3. Line 141: We iterate over conditions, and `--x123` is one of them
4. Line 146: The keyPath becomes `[key, condition]` which is `['color', '--x123']`

So defineConsts placeholders only appear as conditions in the keyPath, not as properties. This means our filter should be correct. However, there's a subtle issue: what if someone writes:

```javascript
{
  color: {
    '--my-manual-var': 'red',  // This is NOT a defineConsts placeholder
    default: 'blue'
  }
}
```

This would be invalid CSS but our code might process it. Let me check if the validation catches this. Looking at the validation code in basic-validation.js, line 61-72:

```javascript
if (
  !(
    key.startsWith('@') ||
    key.startsWith(':') ||
    key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    key.startsWith('--') ||  // We added this
    key === 'default'
  )
) {
  throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
}
```

With our change, a key like `'--my-manual-var'` would pass validation. But this might actually be intentional - if someone wants to use a CSS variable name as a condition key, they can. The browser would just ignore it as invalid CSS. So our fix is correct.

However, I realize we need to be more careful. The issue is that `key.startsWith('--')` is very broad. Let me reconsider. Looking at line 47-49 again:

```javascript
const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
  ? _key.slice(4, -1)
  : _key;
```

The regex `/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/` only matches very specific patterns: `var(--<alphanumeric>)`. This is the pattern used by defineConsts. So after stripping, we get `--<alphanumeric>`.

A user-written CSS variable could be something like `--my-custom-var` (with hyphens), which wouldn't match the regex pattern, so it wouldn't get stripped. Let me verify this understanding:

- `var(--x1r2wpmh)` matches the regex, becomes `--x1r2wpmh`
- `var(--my-custom-var)` does NOT match the regex (because of the hyphen), stays as `var(--my-custom-var)`

So the validation should check for:
- `key.startsWith('var(--')` - for non-stripped defineConsts placeholders or user variables
- `key.startsWith('--') && /^--[a-z0-9]+$/.test(key)` - for stripped defineConsts placeholders

But this might be too strict. Let me look at what happens in practice. Let me check if there are tests for CSS variables as property names:

I see the issue! In this test, `--background-color` and `--otherColor` are CSS property names (in the top-level of the style object), not condition keys. The problem is that in the PreRule's `constRules` method, we're now also including keys that start with `--` which includes actual CSS property names that happen to start with `--`.

The issue is that we need to distinguish between:
1. `--x123` as a condition key (from defineConsts, after var() stripping)
2. `--background-color` as a CSS property name

Looking at the regex pattern in flatten-raw-style-obj.js line 47:
```javascript
const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
  ? _key.slice(4, -1)
  : _key;
```

The regex `/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/` matches `var(--x123)` but not `var(--background-color)` (because of the hyphen). So:
- `var(--x1r2wpmh)` (defineConsts placeholder) → becomes `--x1r2wpmh`
- `--background-color` (CSS property) → stays as `--background-color`

So the pattern for stripped defineConsts placeholders is `--[a-z0-9]+` (no hyphens). Let me update the validation and PreRule to use this more specific pattern:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js   --old_str 'function validateConditionalStyles(
  val: ConditionalStyles,
  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
): void {
  for (const key in val) {
    const v = val[key];
    if (
      !(
        key.startsWith('"'"'@'"'"') ||
        key.startsWith('"'"':'"'"') ||
        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
        key.startsWith('"'"'var(--'"'"') ||

        key.startsWith('"'"'--'"'"') ||
        key === '"'"'default'"'"'

      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    }

  val: ConditionalStyles,

      !(
        key.startsWith('"'"'@'"'"') ||
        key.startsWith('"'"':'"'"') ||
        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined

    60	        if (value === null) {
    61	          flattened.push([property, new NullPreRule()]);
    62	        } else {
    63	          flattened.push([
    64	            property,
    65	            new PreRule(
    66	              property,
    67	              value,
    68	              keyPath.includes(key)
    69	                ? keyPath.map((k) => (k === key ? property : k))
    70	                : [...keyPath, property],
    71	            ),
    72	          ]);
    73	        }
    74	      }
    75	      continue;
    76	    }

   161	function evaluateThemeRef(
   162	  fileName: string,
   163	  exportName: string,
   164	  state: State,
   165	): { [key: string]: string } {
   166	  const resolveKey = (key: string) => {
   167	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
   168	      return `var(${key})`;
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    const strToHash =
   172	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   173	        ? utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName })
   174	        : utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName, key });
   175	
   176	    const { debug, enableDebugClassNames } = state.traversalState.options;
   177	
   178	    const varSafeKey =
   179	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   180	        ? ''
   181	        : (key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key).replace(
   182	            /[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,
   183	            '_',
   184	          ) + '-';
   185	
   186	    const varName =
   187	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
   188	        ? varSafeKey +
   189	          state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix +
   190	          utils.hash(strToHash)
   191	        : state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix + utils.hash(strToHash);
   192	
   193	    if (key === '__varGroupHash__') {
   194	      return varName;
   195	    }
   196	    return `var(--${varName})`;
   197	  };
   198	
   199	  // A JS proxy that uses the key to generate a string value using the `resolveKey` function
   200	  const proxy = new Proxy(
   201	    {},
   202	    {
   203	      get(_, key: string) {
   204	        return resolveKey(key);
   205	      },
   206	      set(_, key: string, value: string) {
   207	        throw new Error(
   208	          `Cannot set value ${value} to key ${key} in theme ${fileName}`,
   209	        );
   210	      },
   211	    },
   212	  );
   213	
   214	  return proxy;
   215	}

Aha! There it is! In `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively` at lines 153-155, if a key starts with `var(` and ends with `)`, it strips off those wrappers! This is separate from the stripping in flatten-raw-style-obj.js.

So for dynamic functions, the key stripping happens during the evaluation phase (in parse-stylex-create-arg.js), and then the object gets validated. This is why we see `--x1r2wpmh` in the validation.

So our fix is correct - we need to check for keys that match the pattern of stripped defineConsts placeholders. But the question is: what's the correct pattern?

Looking at line 153, the check is `key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')`, which is very broad and would match any key like `var(anything)`. But in practice, defineConsts placeholders come from the evaluateThemeRef function, which generates keys like `var(--x<hash>)`.

So let me think about the safest approach:
1. User CSS variables won't start with `var(` - they'd just be `--my-var`
2. defineConsts placeholders after stripping would be `--x<hash>` or similar

Actually, wait. Let me reconsider. Looking at the regex in flatten-raw-style-obj.js:
```javascript
const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
  ? _key.slice(4, -1)
  : _key;
```

This regex is very specific: `/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/`. It matches `var(--` followed by only lowercase letters and digits, then `)`. No hyphens, no uppercase, no underscores.

But in parse-stylex-create-arg.js:
```javascript
if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
  key = key.slice(4, -1);
}
```

This is much broader! It strips `var()` from ANY key that has that pattern, not just the specific defineConsts pattern.

So the issue is that the stripping logic is inconsistent between the two places. The solution is either:
1. Make parse-stylex-create-arg.js use the same specific regex as flatten-raw-style-obj.js
2. Make the validation recognize the broader pattern

Looking at the existing comment in the validation code, it says "This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined". So the intent is specifically for defineConsts values, not for any arbitrary `var()` expression.

Therefore, I think we should:
1. Use the same specific regex in parse-stylex-create-arg.js
2. Make the validation recognize the specific pattern

Let me update parse-stylex-create-arg.js to use the same regex:

// This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined

Actually, let me double-check this. Let me look at what values are actually being validated. Let me trace through the flow again:

1. In `evaluateStyleXCreateArg` (parse-stylex-create-arg.js), we evaluate the arrow function body
2. For dynamic functions, we call `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively` which strips `var()` wrappers
3. The resulting object is returned to `transformStyleXCreate` (stylex-create.js)
4. Then `stylexCreate(plainObject, state.options)` is called (line 211 in stylex-create.js)
5. Inside `styleXCreateSet` (stylex-create.js), `validateNamespace(namespace)` is called (line 57)

So the validation runs on the object that was already processed by `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively`, which means the keys are already stripped!

Now I understand. The check `key.startsWith('var(--')` was meant to handle non-stripped keys, but in the dynamic function case, the keys are already stripped before validation. So we need both checks:
- `key.startsWith('var(--')` for non-stripped keys (static case)
- A pattern for stripped keys (dynamic case)

For the stripped pattern, since we can't know the classNamePrefix, we should accept any key that matches the defineConsts placeholder pattern after stripping. The regex `/^var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)$/` strips to `--[a-z0-9]+`, so we should check for `/^--[a-z0-9]+$/`.

But this brings us back to the collision problem with `--foo`. However, I think the collision is actually acceptable, because:
1. Using `--foo` as a condition key (not as a property) would be unusual
2. defineConsts placeholders are designed to have unique hashes

Actually, let me verify what a user would write. If they write:

```javascript
{
  color: {
    '--foo': 'red',  // Is this valid?
    default: 'blue'
  }
}
```

Would this be valid CSS? No! CSS custom properties can only be set as properties, not as conditions. So `'--foo'` as a condition key doesn't make sense in CSS.

Therefore, it's safe to assume that any key matching `/^--[a-z0-9]+$/` in a conditional context is a defineConsts placeholder, not a user CSS variable. User CSS variables would only appear as property keys, not condition keys.

So our original fix of using `/^--[a-z0-9]+$/` is correct. The test failures we're seeing must be due to something else. Let me rebuild and run the tests again:

2025-12-26 16:09:48,934 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
I see! The issue is that the CSS property `--x1anmu0j` is being treated as a condition (priority 2) instead of a property (priority 1), and it's generating a different CSS structure. The CSS rule is being wrapped in `--x1anmu0j{...}` instead of being a simple `.x1b33ekn{...}`.

This confirms my suspicion that our regex `/^--[a-z0-9]+$/` is too broad and is matching actual CSS property names that happen to be generated by defineVars.

The key insight is that:
- CSS variable names from `defineVars` would be like `--x1mxfvjx` (with the classNamePrefix `x`)
- CSS variable placeholders from `defineConsts` would be like `--x1r2wpmh` (also with the classNamePrefix `x`)

They have the same pattern! So we can't distinguish between them using just the pattern.

The difference is in the context:
- CSS variable names from defineVars appear as PROPERTY keys (e.g., `{ '--x1mxfvjx': 500 }`)
- CSS variable placeholders from defineConsts appear as CONDITION keys (e.g., `{ color: { '--x1r2wpmh': 'red' } }`)

And the validation in `validateConditionalStyles` only runs on condition keys, not property keys! So the validation should be safe.

But the issue is in the PreRule's `constRules()` method. That method is being called on ALL rules, including those where `--x1anmu0j` is a property, not a condition.

Let me look at the PreRule's keyPath more carefully. If we have:

```javascript
{
  '--x1anmu0j': 500
}
```

The keyPath would be `['--x1anmu0j']`. And if we have:

```javascript
{
  color: {
    '--x1r2wpmh': 'red'
  }
}
```

The keyPath would be `['color', '--x1r2wpmh']`.

So in the first case, `--x1anmu0j` is the property itself (first element of keyPath). In the second case, `--x1r2wpmh` is a condition (not the first element).

So we should only treat a `--<alphanumeric>` key as a constRule if it's NOT the first element in the keyPath:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/src/shared/preprocess-rules/PreRule.js   --old_str '  get constRules(): $ReadOnlyArray<string> {
    // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    // After flattening, var(--xyz) becomes --xyz (where xyz follows the pattern x<alphanumeric>)
    // This pattern matches defineConsts placeholders but not user CSS variable names
    return this.keyPath.filter((key) => key.startsWith('"'"'var(--'"'"') || /^--x[a-z0-9]+$/.test(key));

    // we check that the key is not at index 0 (i.e., it'"'"'s a condition, not a property name)
    return this.keyPath.filter((key, index) =>
